36 class RefinedPrinter(_ctx: Context) extends PlainPrinter(_ctx) {
37 
38   /** A stack of enclosing DefDef, TypeDef, or ClassDef, or ModuleDefs nodes */
39   private[this] var enclosingDef: untpd.Tree = untpd.EmptyTree
40   private[this] var myCtx: Context = _ctx
41   private[this] var printPos = ctx.settings.YprintPos.value
42   private[this] val printLines = ctx.settings.printLines.value
43 
44   override protected[this] implicit def ctx: Context = myCtx
45 
46   def withEnclosingDef(enclDef: Tree[_ >: Untyped])(op: => Text): Text = {
47     val savedCtx = myCtx
48     if (enclDef.hasType && enclDef.symbol.exists)
49       myCtx = ctx.withOwner(enclDef.symbol)
50     val savedDef = enclosingDef
51     enclosingDef = enclDef
52     try op finally {
53       myCtx = savedCtx
54       enclosingDef = savedDef
55     }
56   }
57 
58   def inPattern(op: => Text): Text = {
59     val savedCtx = myCtx
60     myCtx = ctx.addMode(Mode.Pattern)
61     try op finally myCtx = savedCtx
62   }
63 
64   def withoutPos(op: => Text): Text = {
65     val savedPrintPos = printPos
66     printPos = false
67     try op finally printPos = savedPrintPos
68   }
69 
70   protected def enclDefIsClass = enclosingDef match {
71     case owner: TypeDef => owner.isClassDef
72     case owner: untpd.ModuleDef => true
73     case _ => false
74   }
75 
76   override protected def recursionLimitExceeded() = {}
77 
78   protected val PrintableFlags = (SourceModifierFlags | Label | Module | Local).toCommonFlags
79 
80   override def nameString(name: Name): String =
81     if (ctx.settings.YdebugNames.value) name.debugString else name.toString
82 
83   override protected def simpleNameString(sym: Symbol): String =
84     nameString(if (ctx.property(XprintMode).isEmpty) sym.originalName else sym.name)
85 
86   override def fullNameString(sym: Symbol): String =
87     if (isEmptyPrefix(sym.maybeOwner)) nameString(sym)
88     else super.fullNameString(sym)
89 
90   override protected def fullNameOwner(sym: Symbol) = {
91     val owner = super.fullNameOwner(sym)
92     if (owner is ModuleClass) owner.sourceModule else owner
93   }
94 
95   override def toTextRef(tp: SingletonType): Text = controlled {
96     tp match {
97       case tp: ThisType =>
98         if (tp.cls.isAnonymousClass) return keywordStr("this")
99         if (tp.cls is ModuleClass) return fullNameString(tp.cls.sourceModule)
100       case _ =>
101     }
102     super.toTextRef(tp)
103   }
104 
105   override def toTextPrefix(tp: Type): Text = controlled {
106     def isOmittable(sym: Symbol) =
107       if (ctx.settings.verbose.value) false
108       else if (homogenizedView) isEmptyPrefix(sym) // drop <root> and anonymous classes, but not scala, Predef.
109       else isOmittablePrefix(sym)
110     tp match {
111       case tp: ThisType =>
112         if (isOmittable(tp.cls)) return ""
113       case tp @ TermRef(pre, _) =>
114         val sym = tp.symbol
115         if (sym.isPackageObject) return toTextPrefix(pre)
116         if (isOmittable(sym)) return ""
117       case _ =>
118     }
119     super.toTextPrefix(tp)
120   }
121 
122   override protected def refinementNameString(tp: RefinedType): String =
123     if (tp.parent.isInstanceOf[WildcardType] || tp.refinedName == nme.WILDCARD)
124       super.refinementNameString(tp)
125     else {
126       val tsym = tp.parent.member(tp.refinedName).symbol
127       if (!tsym.exists) super.refinementNameString(tp)
128       else simpleNameString(tsym)
129     }
130 
131   override def toText(tp: Type): Text = controlled {
132     def toTextTuple(args: List[Type]): Text =
133       "(" ~ Text(args.map(argText), ", ") ~ ")"
134 
135     def toTextFunction(args: List[Type], isImplicit: Boolean): Text =
136       changePrec(GlobalPrec) {
137         val argStr: Text =
138           if (args.length == 2 && !defn.isTupleType(args.head))
139             atPrec(InfixPrec) { argText(args.head) }
140           else
141             toTextTuple(args.init)
142         (keywordText("implicit ") provided isImplicit) ~ argStr ~ " => " ~ argText(args.last)
143       }
144 
145     def toTextDependentFunction(appType: MethodType): Text = {
146       (keywordText("implicit ") provided appType.isImplicitMethod) ~
147       "(" ~ paramsText(appType) ~ ") => " ~ toText(appType.resultType)
148     }
149 
150     def isInfixType(tp: Type): Boolean = tp match {
151       case AppliedType(tycon, args) =>
152         args.length == 2 &&
153         tycon.typeSymbol.getAnnotation(defn.ShowAsInfixAnnot).map(_.argumentConstant(0).forall(_.booleanValue))
154           .getOrElse(!Character.isUnicodeIdentifierStart(tycon.typeSymbol.name.toString.head))
155       case _ => false
156     }
157 
158     def toTextInfixType(op: Type, args: List[Type]): Text = {
159       /* SLS 3.2.8: all infix types have the same precedence.
160        * In A op B op' C, op and op' need the same associativity.
161        * Therefore, if op is left associative, anything on its right
162        * needs to be parenthesized if it's an infix type, and vice versa. */
163       val l :: r :: Nil = args
164       val isRightAssoc = op.typeSymbol.name.endsWith(":")
165       val leftArg = if (isRightAssoc && isInfixType(l)) "(" ~ argText(l) ~ ")" else argText(l)
166       val rightArg = if (!isRightAssoc && isInfixType(r)) "(" ~ argText(r) ~ ")" else argText(r)
167 
168       leftArg ~ " " ~ toTextLocal(op) ~ " " ~ rightArg
169     }
170 
171     homogenize(tp) match {
172       case x: ConstantType if homogenizedView =>
173         return toText(x.widen)
174       case AppliedType(tycon, args) =>
175         val cls = tycon.typeSymbol
176         if (tycon.isRepeatedParam) return toTextLocal(args.head) ~ "*"
177         if (defn.isFunctionClass(cls)) return toTextFunction(args, cls.name.isImplicitFunction)
178         if (defn.isTupleClass(cls)) return toTextTuple(args)
179         if (isInfixType(tp)) return toTextInfixType(tycon, args)
180       case EtaExpansion(tycon) =>
181         return toText(tycon)
182       case tp: RefinedType if defn.isFunctionType(tp) =>
183         return toTextDependentFunction(tp.refinedInfo.asInstanceOf[MethodType])
184       case tp: TypeRef =>
185         if (tp.symbol.isAnonymousClass && !ctx.settings.uniqid.value)
186           return toText(tp.info)
187         if (tp.symbol.is(Param))
188           tp.prefix match {
189             case pre: ThisType if pre.cls == tp.symbol.owner =>
190               return nameString(tp.symbol)
191             case _ =>
192           }
193       case tp: ExprType =>
194         return exprToText(tp)
195       case ErasedValueType(tycon, underlying) =>
196         return "ErasedValueType(" ~ toText(tycon) ~ ", " ~ toText(underlying) ~ ")"
197       case tp: ClassInfo =>
198         return toTextParents(tp.parents) ~ "{...}"
199       case JavaArrayType(elemtp) =>
200         return toText(elemtp) ~ "[]"
201       case tp: AnnotatedType if homogenizedView =>
202         // Positions of annotations in types are not serialized
203         // (they don't need to because we keep the original type tree with
204         //  the original annotation anyway. Therefore, there will always be
205         //  one version of the annotation tree that has the correct positions).
206         withoutPos(super.toText(tp))
207       case tp: SelectionProto =>
208         return "?{ " ~ toText(tp.name) ~
209            (Str(" ") provided !tp.name.toSimpleName.last.isLetterOrDigit) ~
210            ": " ~ toText(tp.memberProto) ~ " }"
211       case tp: ViewProto =>
212         return toText(tp.argType) ~ " ?=>? " ~ toText(tp.resultType)
213       case tp @ FunProto(args, resultType, _) =>
214         val argsText = args match {
215           case dummyTreeOfType(tp) :: Nil if !(tp isRef defn.NullClass) => "null: " ~ toText(tp)
216           case _ => toTextGlobal(args, ", ")
217         }
218         return "FunProto(" ~ argsText ~ "):" ~ toText(resultType)
219       case tp: IgnoredProto =>
220         return "?"
221       case _ =>
222     }
223     super.toText(tp)
224   }
225 
226   protected def exprToText(tp: ExprType): Text =
227     "=> " ~ toText(tp.resType)
228 
229   protected def blockText[T >: Untyped](trees: List[Tree[T]]): Text =
230     ("{" ~ toText(trees, "\n") ~ "}").close
231 
232   override def toText[T >: Untyped](tree: Tree[T]): Text = controlled {
233     import untpd.{modsDeco => _, _}
234 
235     def isLocalThis(tree: Tree) = tree.typeOpt match {
236       case tp: ThisType => tp.cls == ctx.owner.enclosingClass
237       case _ => false
238     }
239 
240     def optDotPrefix(tree: This) = optText(tree.qual)(_ ~ ".") provided !isLocalThis(tree)
241 
242     def caseBlockText(tree: Tree): Text = tree match {
243       case Block(stats, expr) => toText(stats :+ expr, "\n")
244       case expr => toText(expr)
245     }
246 
247     // Dotty deviation: called with an untpd.Tree, so cannot be a untpd.Tree[T] (seems to be a Scala2 problem to allow this)
248     // More deviations marked below as // DD
249     def enumText(tree: untpd.Tree) = tree match { // DD
250       case _: untpd.GenFrom | _: untpd.GenAlias => toText(tree)
251       case _ => keywordStr("if ") ~ toText(tree)
252     }
253 
254     def forText(enums: List[untpd.Tree], expr: untpd.Tree, sep: String): Text = // DD
255       changePrec(GlobalPrec) { keywordStr("for ") ~ Text(enums map enumText, "; ") ~ sep ~ toText(expr) }
256 
257     def cxBoundToText(bound: untpd.Tree): Text = bound match { // DD
258       case AppliedTypeTree(tpt, _) => " : " ~ toText(tpt)
259       case untpd.Function(_, tpt) => " <% " ~ toText(tpt)
260     }
261 
262     def varianceText(mods: untpd.Modifiers) =
263       if (mods is Covariant) "+"
264       else if (mods is Contravariant) "-"
265       else ""
266 
267     def argText(arg: Tree): Text = arg match {
268       case arg: TypeBoundsTree => "_" ~ toTextGlobal(arg)
269       case arg: TypeTree =>
270         arg.typeOpt match {
271           case tp: TypeBounds => "_" ~ toTextGlobal(arg)
272           case _ => toTextGlobal(arg)
273         }
274       case _ => toTextGlobal(arg)
275     }
276 
277     def toTextCore(tree: Tree): Text = tree match {
278       case id: Trees.BackquotedIdent[_] if !homogenizedView =>
279         "`" ~ toText(id.name) ~ "`"
280       case id: Trees.SearchFailureIdent[_] =>
281         tree.typeOpt match {
282           case reason: Implicits.SearchFailureType =>
283             toText(id.name) ~ "implicitly[" ~ toText(reason.expectedType) ~ "]"
284           case _ =>
285             toText(id.name)
286         }
287       case Ident(name) =>
288         val txt = tree.typeOpt match {
289           case tp: NamedType if name != nme.WILDCARD =>
290             val pre = if (tp.symbol is JavaStatic) tp.prefix.widen else tp.prefix
291             toTextPrefix(pre) ~ withPos(selectionString(tp), tree.pos)
292           case _ =>
293             toText(name)
294         }
295         if (name.isTypeName) typeText(txt)
296         else txt
297       case tree @ Select(qual, name) =>
298         if (qual.isType) toTextLocal(qual) ~ "#" ~ typeText(toText(name))
299         else toTextLocal(qual) ~ ("." ~ nameIdText(tree) provided name != nme.CONSTRUCTOR)
300       case tree: This =>
301         optDotPrefix(tree) ~ keywordStr("this") ~ idText(tree)
302       case Super(qual: This, mix) =>
303         optDotPrefix(qual) ~ keywordStr("super") ~ optText(mix)("[" ~ _ ~ "]")
304       case Apply(fun, args) =>
305         if (fun.hasType && fun.symbol == defn.throwMethod)
306           changePrec (GlobalPrec) {
307             keywordStr("throw ") ~ toText(args.head)
308           }
309         else
310           toTextLocal(fun) ~ "(" ~ toTextGlobal(args, ", ") ~ ")"
311       case TypeApply(fun, args) =>
312         toTextLocal(fun) ~ "[" ~ toTextGlobal(args, ", ") ~ "]"
313       case Literal(c) =>
314         tree.typeOpt match {
315           case ConstantType(tc) => withPos(toText(tc), tree.pos)
316           case _ => withPos(toText(c), tree.pos)
317         }
318       case New(tpt) =>
319         keywordStr("new ") ~ {
320           tpt match {
321             case tpt: Template => toTextTemplate(tpt, ofNew = true)
322             case _ =>
323               if (tpt.hasType)
324                 toTextLocal(tpt.typeOpt.underlyingClassRef(refinementOK = false))
325               else
326                 toTextLocal(tpt)
327           }
328         }
329       case Typed(expr, tpt) =>
330         changePrec(InfixPrec) { toText(expr) ~ ": " ~ toText(tpt) }
331       case NamedArg(name, arg) =>
332         toText(name) ~ " = " ~ toText(arg)
333       case Assign(lhs, rhs) =>
334         changePrec(GlobalPrec) { toTextLocal(lhs) ~ " = " ~ toText(rhs) }
335       case Block(stats, expr) =>
336         blockText(stats :+ expr)
337       case If(cond, thenp, elsep) =>
338         changePrec(GlobalPrec) {
339           keywordStr("if ") ~ toText(cond) ~ (keywordText(" then") provided !cond.isInstanceOf[Parens]) ~~ toText(thenp) ~ optText(elsep)(keywordStr(" else ") ~ _)
340         }
341       case Closure(env, ref, target) =>
342         "closure(" ~ (toTextGlobal(env, ", ") ~ " | " provided env.nonEmpty) ~
343         toTextGlobal(ref) ~ (":" ~ toText(target) provided !target.isEmpty) ~ ")"
344       case Match(sel, cases) =>
345         if (sel.isEmpty) blockText(cases)
346         else changePrec(GlobalPrec) { toText(sel) ~ keywordStr(" match ") ~ blockText(cases) }
347       case CaseDef(pat, guard, body) =>
348         keywordStr("case ") ~ inPattern(toText(pat)) ~ optText(guard)(keywordStr(" if ") ~ _) ~ " => " ~ caseBlockText(body)
349       case Return(expr, from) =>
350         changePrec(GlobalPrec) { keywordStr("return") ~ optText(expr)(" " ~ _) }
351       case Try(expr, cases, finalizer) =>
352         changePrec(GlobalPrec) {
353           keywordStr("try ") ~ toText(expr) ~ optText(cases)(keywordStr(" catch ") ~ _) ~ optText(finalizer)(keywordStr(" finally ") ~ _)
354         }
355       case Throw(expr) =>
356         changePrec(GlobalPrec) {
357           keywordStr("throw ") ~ toText(expr)
358         }
359       case SeqLiteral(elems, elemtpt) =>
360         "[" ~ toTextGlobal(elems, ",") ~ " : " ~ toText(elemtpt) ~ "]"
361       case tree @ Inlined(call, bindings, body) =>
362         (("/* inlined from " ~ toText(call) ~ "*/ ") provided !homogenizedView) ~
363         blockText(bindings :+ body)
364       case tpt: untpd.DerivedTypeTree =>
365         "<derived typetree watching " ~ summarized(toText(tpt.watched)) ~ ">"
366       case TypeTree() =>
367         typeText(toText(tree.typeOpt))
368       case SingletonTypeTree(ref) =>
369         toTextLocal(ref) ~ "." ~ keywordStr("type")
370       case AndTypeTree(l, r) =>
371         changePrec(AndPrec) { toText(l) ~ " & " ~ toText(r) }
372       case OrTypeTree(l, r) =>
373         changePrec(OrPrec) { toText(l) ~ " | " ~ toText(r) }
374       case RefinedTypeTree(tpt, refines) =>
375         toTextLocal(tpt) ~ " " ~ blockText(refines)
376       case AppliedTypeTree(tpt, args) =>
377         toTextLocal(tpt) ~ "[" ~ Text(args map argText, ", ") ~ "]"
378       case LambdaTypeTree(tparams, body) =>
379         changePrec(GlobalPrec) {
380           tparamsText(tparams) ~ " -> " ~ toText(body)
381         }
382       case ByNameTypeTree(tpt) =>
383         "=> " ~ toTextLocal(tpt)
384       case TypeBoundsTree(lo, hi) =>
385         if (lo eq hi) optText(lo)(" = " ~ _)
386         else optText(lo)(" >: " ~ _) ~ optText(hi)(" <: " ~ _)
387       case Bind(name, body) =>
388         changePrec(InfixPrec) { toText(name) ~ " @ " ~ toText(body) }
389       case Alternative(trees) =>
390         changePrec(OrPrec) { toText(trees, " | ") }
391       case UnApply(fun, implicits, patterns) =>
392         val extractor = fun match {
393           case Select(extractor, nme.unapply) => extractor
394           case _ => fun
395         }
396         toTextLocal(extractor) ~
397         "(" ~ toTextGlobal(patterns, ", ") ~ ")" ~
398         ("(" ~ toTextGlobal(implicits, ", ") ~ ")" provided implicits.nonEmpty)
399       case tree @ ValDef(_, _, _) =>
400         valDefToText(tree)
401       case tree @ DefDef(_, _, _, _, _) =>
402         defDefToText(tree)
403       case tree @ TypeDef(name, rhs) =>
404         def typeDefText(tparamsText: => Text, rhsText: => Text) =
405           dclTextOr(tree) {
406             modText(tree.mods, keywordStr("type")) ~~ (varianceText(tree.mods) ~ typeText(nameIdText(tree))) ~
407             withEnclosingDef(tree) { tparamsText ~ rhsText }
408           }
409         def recur(rhs: Tree, tparamsTxt: => Text): Text = rhs match {
410           case impl: Template =>
411             templateText(tree, impl)
412           case rhs: TypeBoundsTree =>
413             typeDefText(tparamsTxt, toText(rhs))
414           case LambdaTypeTree(tparams, body) =>
415             recur(body, tparamsText(tparams))
416           case rhs: TypeTree if rhs.typeOpt.isInstanceOf[TypeBounds] =>
417             typeDefText(tparamsTxt, toText(rhs))
418           case rhs =>
419             typeDefText(tparamsTxt, optText(rhs)(" = " ~ _))
420         }
421         recur(rhs, "")
422       case Import(expr, selectors) =>
423         def selectorText(sel: Tree): Text = sel match {
424           case Thicket(l :: r :: Nil) => toTextGlobal(l) ~ " => " ~ toTextGlobal(r)
425           case _ => toTextGlobal(sel)
426         }
427         val selectorsText: Text = selectors match {
428           case id :: Nil => toText(id)
429           case _ => "{" ~ Text(selectors map selectorText, ", ") ~ "}"
430         }
431         keywordStr("import ") ~ toTextLocal(expr) ~ "." ~ selectorsText
432       case packageDef: PackageDef =>
433         packageDefText(packageDef)
434       case tree: Template =>
435         toTextTemplate(tree)
436       case Annotated(arg, annot) =>
437         toTextLocal(arg) ~~ annotText(annot)
438       case EmptyTree =>
439         "<empty>"
440       case TypedSplice(t) =>
441         toText(t)
442       case tree @ ModuleDef(name, impl) =>
443         withEnclosingDef(tree) {
444           modText(tree.mods, keywordStr("object")) ~~ nameIdText(tree) ~ toTextTemplate(impl)
445         }
446       case SymbolLit(str) =>
447         "'" + str
448       case InterpolatedString(id, segments) =>
449         def strText(str: Literal) = withPos(escapedString(str.const.stringValue), tree.pos)
450         def segmentText(segment: Tree) = segment match {
451           case Thicket(List(str: Literal, expr)) => strText(str) ~ "{" ~ toTextGlobal(expr) ~ "}"
452           case str: Literal => strText(str)
453         }
454         toText(id) ~ "\"" ~ Text(segments map segmentText, "") ~ "\""
455       case Function(args, body) =>
456         var implicitSeen: Boolean = false
457         def argToText(arg: Tree) = arg match {
458           case arg @ ValDef(name, tpt, _) =>
459             val implicitText =
460               if ((arg.mods is Implicit) && !implicitSeen) { implicitSeen = true; keywordStr("implicit ") }
461               else ""
462             implicitText ~ toText(name) ~ optAscription(tpt)
463           case _ =>
464             toText(arg)
465         }
466         val argsText = args match {
467           case (arg @ ValDef(_, tpt, _)) :: Nil if tpt.isEmpty => argToText(arg)
468           case _ => "(" ~ Text(args map argToText, ", ") ~ ")"
469         }
470         changePrec(GlobalPrec) {
471           argsText ~ " => " ~ toText(body)
472         }
473       case InfixOp(l, op, r) =>
474         val opPrec = parsing.precedence(op.name)
475         changePrec(opPrec) { toText(l) ~ " " ~ toText(op) ~ " " ~ toText(r) }
476       case PostfixOp(l, op) =>
477         changePrec(InfixPrec) { toText(l) ~ " " ~ toText(op) }
478       case PrefixOp(op, r) =>
479         changePrec(DotPrec) { toText(op) ~ " " ~ toText(r) }
480       case Parens(t) =>
481         "(" ~ toTextGlobal(t) ~ ")"
482       case Tuple(ts) =>
483         "(" ~ toTextGlobal(ts, ", ") ~ ")"
484       case WhileDo(cond, body) =>
485         changePrec(GlobalPrec) { keywordStr("while ") ~ toText(cond) ~ keywordStr(" do ") ~ toText(body) }
486       case DoWhile(cond, body) =>
487         changePrec(GlobalPrec) { keywordStr("do ") ~ toText(body) ~ keywordStr(" while ") ~ toText(cond) }
488       case ForYield(enums, expr) =>
489         forText(enums, expr, keywordStr(" yield "))
490       case ForDo(enums, expr) =>
491         forText(enums, expr, keywordStr(" do "))
492       case GenFrom(pat, expr) =>
493         toText(pat) ~ " <- " ~ toText(expr)
494       case GenAlias(pat, expr) =>
495         toText(pat) ~ " = " ~ toText(expr)
496       case ContextBounds(bounds, cxBounds) =>
497         (toText(bounds) /: cxBounds) {(t, cxb) =>
498           t ~ cxBoundToText(cxb)
499         }
500       case PatDef(mods, pats, tpt, rhs) =>
501         modText(mods, keywordStr("val")) ~~ toText(pats, ", ") ~ optAscription(tpt) ~
502           optText(rhs)(" = " ~ _)
503       case ParsedTry(expr, handler, finalizer) =>
504         changePrec(GlobalPrec) {
505           keywordStr("try ") ~ toText(expr) ~ " " ~ keywordStr("catch") ~ " {" ~ toText(handler) ~ "}" ~ optText(finalizer)(keywordStr(" finally ") ~ _)
506         }
507       case Quote(tree) =>
508         if (tree.isType) "'[" ~ toTextGlobal(tree) ~ "]" else "'(" ~ toTextGlobal(tree) ~ ")"
509       case Thicket(trees) =>
510         "Thicket {" ~~ toTextGlobal(trees, "\n") ~~ "}"
511       case _ =>
512         tree.fallbackToText(this)
513     }
514 
515     var txt = toTextCore(tree)
516 
517     def suppressTypes =
518       tree.isType || tree.isDef || // don't print types of types or defs
519       homogenizedView && ctx.mode.is(Mode.Pattern)
520         // When comparing pickled info, disregard types of patterns.
521         // The reason is that GADT matching can rewrite types of pattern trees
522         // without changing the trees themselves. (see Typer.typedCase.indexPatterns.transform).
523         // But then pickling and unpickling the original trees will yield trees
524         // with the original types before they are rewritten, which causes a discrepancy.
525 
526     def suppressPositions = tree match {
527       case _: WithoutTypeOrPos[_] | _: TypeTree => true // TypeTrees never have an interesting position
528       case _ => false
529     }
530 
531     if (ctx.settings.XprintTypes.value && tree.hasType) {
532       // add type to term nodes; replace type nodes with their types unless -Yprint-pos is also set.
533       def tp = tree.typeOpt match {
534         case tp: TermRef if tree.isInstanceOf[RefTree] && !tp.denot.isOverloaded => tp.underlying
535         case tp => tp
536       }
537       if (!suppressTypes)
538         txt = ("<" ~ txt ~ ":" ~ toText(tp) ~ ">").close
539       else if (tree.isType && !homogenizedView)
540         txt = toText(tp)
541     }
542     if (!suppressPositions) {
543       if (printPos) {
544         val pos =
545           if (homogenizedView && !tree.isInstanceOf[MemberDef]) tree.pos.toSynthetic
546           else tree.pos
547         val clsStr = ""//if (tree.isType) tree.getClass.toString else ""
548         txt = (txt ~ "@" ~ pos.toString ~ clsStr).close
549       }
550       if (ctx.settings.YprintPosSyms.value && tree.isDef)
551         txt = (txt ~
552           s"@@(${tree.symbol.name}=" ~ tree.symbol.pos.toString ~ ")").close
553    }
554     if (ctx.settings.YshowTreeIds.value)
555       txt = (txt ~ "#" ~ tree.uniqueId.toString).close
556     tree match {
557       case Block(_, _) | Template(_, _, _, _) => txt
558       case _ => txt.close
559     }
560   }
561 
562   /** Print modifiers from symbols if tree has type, overriding the untpd behavior. */
563   implicit def modsDeco(mdef: untpd.MemberDef)(implicit ctx: Context): untpd.ModsDecorator =
564     new untpd.ModsDecorator {
565       def mods = if (mdef.hasType) Modifiers(mdef.symbol) else mdef.rawMods
566     }
567 
568   def Modifiers(sym: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context): Modifiers = untpd.Modifiers(
569     sym.flags & (if (sym.isType) ModifierFlags | VarianceFlags else ModifierFlags),
570     if (sym.privateWithin.exists) sym.privateWithin.asType.name else tpnme.EMPTY,
571     sym.annotations map (_.tree))
572 
573   protected def optAscription[T >: Untyped](tpt: Tree[T]) = optText(tpt)(": " ~ _)
574 
575   private def idText(tree: untpd.Tree): Text = {
576     if ((ctx.settings.uniqid.value || Printer.debugPrintUnique) && tree.hasType && tree.symbol.exists) s"#${tree.symbol.id}" else ""
577   }
578 
579   private def useSymbol(tree: untpd.Tree) =
580     tree.hasType && tree.symbol.exists && ctx.settings.YprintSyms.value
581 
582   protected def nameIdText[T >: Untyped](tree: NameTree[T]): Text = {
583     if (tree.hasType && tree.symbol.exists) {
584       val str: Text = nameString(tree.symbol)
585       tree match {
586         case tree: RefTree => withPos(str, tree.pos)
587         case tree: MemberDef => withPos(str, tree.namePos)
588         case _ => str
589       }
590     }
591     else toText(tree.name) ~ idText(tree)
592   }
593 
594   protected def dclTextOr[T >: Untyped](tree: Tree[T])(treeText: => Text) =
595     if (useSymbol(tree))
596       annotsText(tree.symbol) ~~ dclText(tree.symbol) ~
597         ( " <in " ~ toText(tree.symbol.owner) ~ ">" provided ctx.settings.YdebugOwners.value)
598     else treeText
599 
600   def tparamsText[T >: Untyped](params: List[Tree[T]]): Text =
601     "[" ~ toText(params, ", ") ~ "]" provided params.nonEmpty
602 
603   def addVparamssText[T >: Untyped](txt: Text, vparamss: List[List[ValDef[T]]]): Text =
604     (txt /: vparamss)((txt, vparams) => txt ~ "(" ~ toText(vparams, ", ") ~ ")")
605 
606   protected def valDefToText[T >: Untyped](tree: ValDef[T]): Text = {
607     import untpd.{modsDeco => _, _}
608     dclTextOr(tree) {
609       modText(tree.mods, keywordStr(if (tree.mods is Mutable) "var" else "val")) ~~
610         valDefText(nameIdText(tree)) ~ optAscription(tree.tpt) ~
611         withEnclosingDef(tree) { optText(tree.rhs)(" = " ~ _) }
612     }
613   }
614 
615   protected def defDefToText[T >: Untyped](tree: DefDef[T]): Text = {
616     import untpd.{modsDeco => _, _}
617     dclTextOr(tree) {
618       val prefix = modText(tree.mods, keywordStr("def")) ~~ valDefText(nameIdText(tree))
619       withEnclosingDef(tree) {
620           addVparamssText(prefix ~ tparamsText(tree.tparams), tree.vparamss) ~ optAscription(tree.tpt) ~
621             optText(tree.rhs)(" = " ~ _)
622       }
623     }
624   }
625 
626   protected def toTextTemplate(impl: Template, ofNew: Boolean = false): Text = {
627     val Template(constr @ DefDef(_, tparams, vparamss, _, _), parents, self, _) = impl
628     val tparamsTxt = withEnclosingDef(constr) { tparamsText(tparams) }
629     val primaryConstrs = if (constr.rhs.isEmpty) Nil else constr :: Nil
630     val prefix: Text =
631       if (vparamss.isEmpty || primaryConstrs.nonEmpty) tparamsTxt
632       else {
633         var modsText = modText(constr.mods, "")
634         if (!modsText.isEmpty) modsText = " " ~ modsText
635         if (constr.mods.hasAnnotations && !constr.mods.hasFlags) modsText = modsText ~~ " this"
636         withEnclosingDef(constr) { addVparamssText(tparamsTxt ~~ modsText, vparamss) }
637       }
638     val parentsText = Text(parents map constrText, keywordStr(" with "))
639     val selfText = {
640       val selfName = if (self.name == nme.WILDCARD) keywordStr("this") else self.name.toString
641       (selfName ~ optText(self.tpt)(": " ~ _) ~ " =>").close
642     } provided !self.isEmpty
643 
644     val body = if (ctx.settings.YtestPickler.value) {
645       // Pickling/unpickling reorders the body members, so we need to homogenize
646       val (params, rest) = impl.body partition {
647         case stat: TypeDef => stat.symbol.is(Param)
648         case stat: ValOrDefDef =>
649           stat.symbol.is(ParamAccessor) && !stat.symbol.isSetter
650         case _ => false
651       }
652       params ::: rest
653     } else impl.body
654 
655     val bodyText = "{" ~~ selfText ~~ toTextGlobal(primaryConstrs ::: body, "\n") ~ "}"
656 
657     prefix ~ (keywordText(" extends") provided !ofNew) ~~ parentsText ~~ bodyText
658   }
659 
660   protected def templateText(tree: TypeDef, impl: Template): Text = {
661     val decl = modText(tree.mods, keywordStr(if ((tree).mods is Trait) "trait" else "class"))
662     decl ~~ typeText(nameIdText(tree)) ~ withEnclosingDef(tree) { toTextTemplate(impl) } ~
663       (if (tree.hasType && ctx.settings.verbose.value) i"[decls = ${tree.symbol.info.decls}]" else "")
664   }
665 
666   protected def toTextPackageId[T >: Untyped](pid: Tree[T]): Text =
667     if (homogenizedView && pid.hasType) toTextLocal(pid.tpe.asInstanceOf[Showable])
668     else toTextLocal(pid)
669 
670   protected def packageDefText(tree: PackageDef): Text = {
671     val statsText = tree.stats match {
672       case (pdef: PackageDef) :: Nil => toText(pdef)
673       case _ => toTextGlobal(tree.stats, "\n")
674     }
675     val bodyText =
676       if (currentPrecedence == TopLevelPrec) "\n" ~ statsText else " {" ~ statsText ~ "}"
677     keywordStr("package ") ~ toTextPackageId(tree.pid) ~ bodyText
678   }
679 
680   protected def constrText(tree: untpd.Tree): Text = toTextLocal(tree).stripPrefix(keywordStr("new ")) // DD
681 
682   protected def annotText(tree: untpd.Tree): Text = "@" ~ constrText(tree) // DD
683 
684   protected def modText(mods: untpd.Modifiers, kw: String): Text = { // DD
685     val suppressKw = if (enclDefIsClass) mods is ParamAndLocal else mods is Param
686     var flagMask =
687       if (ctx.settings.YdebugFlags.value) AnyFlags
688       else if (suppressKw) PrintableFlags &~ Private
689       else PrintableFlags
690     if (homogenizedView && mods.flags.isTypeFlags) flagMask &~= Implicit // drop implicit from classes
691     val flags = mods.flags & flagMask
692     val flagsText = if (flags.isEmpty) "" else keywordStr((mods.flags & flagMask).toString)
693     val annotations = filterModTextAnnots(mods.annotations)
694     Text(annotations.map(annotText), " ") ~~ flagsText ~~ (Str(kw) provided !suppressKw)
695   }
696 
697   protected def filterModTextAnnots(annots: List[untpd.Tree]): List[untpd.Tree] = annots
698 
699   def optText(name: Name)(encl: Text => Text): Text =
700     if (name.isEmpty) "" else encl(toText(name))
701 
702   def optText[T >: Untyped](tree: Tree[T])(encl: Text => Text): Text =
703     if (tree.isEmpty) "" else encl(toText(tree))
704 
705   def optText[T >: Untyped](tree: List[Tree[T]])(encl: Text => Text): Text =
706     if (tree.exists(!_.isEmpty)) encl(blockText(tree)) else ""
707 
708   override protected def ParamRefNameString(name: Name): String =
709     name.invariantName.toString
710 
711   override protected def treatAsTypeParam(sym: Symbol): Boolean = sym is TypeParam
712 
713   override protected def treatAsTypeArg(sym: Symbol) =
714     sym.isType && (sym is ProtectedLocal) &&
715       (sym.allOverriddenSymbols exists (_ is TypeParam))
716 
717   override def toText(sym: Symbol): Text = {
718     if (sym.isImport)
719       sym.infoOrCompleter match {
720         case info: Namer#Completer => return info.original.show
721         case info: ImportType => return s"import $info.expr.show"
722         case _ =>
723       }
724     if (sym.is(ModuleClass))
725       kindString(sym) ~~ (nameString(sym.name.stripModuleClassSuffix) + idString(sym))
726     else
727       super.toText(sym)
728   }
729 
730   override def kindString(sym: Symbol) = {
731     val flags = sym.flagsUNSAFE
732     if (flags is Package) "package"
733     else if (sym.isPackageObject) "package object"
734     else if (flags is Module) "object"
735     else if (flags is ImplClass) "class"
736     else if (sym.isClassConstructor) "constructor"
737     else super.kindString(sym)
738   }
739 
740   override protected def keyString(sym: Symbol): String = {
741     val flags = sym.flagsUNSAFE
742     if (sym.isType && sym.owner.isTerm) ""
743     else if (sym.isPackageObject) "package object"
744     else if (flags.is(Module) && flags.is(Case)) "case object"
745     else if (sym.isClass && flags.is(Case)) "case class"
746     else if (flags is Module) "object"
747     else if (sym.isTerm && !flags.is(Param) && flags.is(Implicit)) "implicit val"
748     else super.keyString(sym)
749   }
750 
751   override def toTextFlags(sym: Symbol) =
752     if (ctx.settings.YdebugFlags.value)
753       super.toTextFlags(sym)
754     else {
755       var flags = sym.flagsUNSAFE
756       if (flags is TypeParam) flags = flags &~ Protected
757       Text((flags & PrintableFlags).flagStrings map (flag => stringToText(keywordStr(flag))), " ")
758     }
759 
760   override def toText(denot: Denotation): Text = denot match {
761     case denot: MultiDenotation => Text(denot.alternatives.map(dclText), " <and> ")
762     case NoDenotation => "NoDenotation"
763     case _ =>
764       if (denot.symbol.exists) toText(denot.symbol)
765       else "some " ~ toText(denot.info)
766   }
767 
768   override def plain = new PlainPrinter(_ctx)
769 
770   private def withPos(txt: Text, pos: SourcePosition): Text = {
771     if (!printLines || !pos.exists) txt
772     else txt match {
773       case Str(s, _) => Str(s, LineRange(pos.line, pos.endLine))
774       case _ => txt
775     }
776   }
